On July 9, 2015, the Chinese government launched a nationwide crackdown on lawyers and rights defenders. More than 300 lawyers & legal associates working on #religiousfreedom and #humanrights cases were detained. As we approach the #thirdanniversary709, we honor these heroes.

KurikoC @kuriko_c
在介绍了人脸识别摄像头的诸多问题（造价高昂远超预算、出错率高、各地数据不共享等）后，Mozur先生表示，这些缺陷正是中国政府夸大自己监控技术能力的原因：不需真正实现监控，只要让人们感到他们处在监控之中，他们的行为就会发生改变，政府即可事实上达到监控目的。

Paul Mozur @paulmozur:
All of these drawbacks are why government has been playing up its tech abilities. You don’t need to be successfully monitoring to influence behaviors. Over and over again we heard about partial surveillance systems changing behaviors as people assumed they were being monitored.

On July 9, 2015, the Chinese government launched a nationwide crackdown on lawyers and rights defenders. More than 300 lawyers & legal associates working on #religiousfreedom and #humanrights cases were detained. As we approach the #thirdanniversary709, we honor these heroes.
